DROP TABLE MEMBER CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE MEMBER (
	ID	VARCHAR2(50)		NOT NULL,
	NAME	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	NICKNAME	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	PWD	VARCHAR2(100)		NULL,
	EMAIL	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	PHONE	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	BIRTHDAY	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	ADDRESS	VARCHAR2(500)		NULL,
	MAIN_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	ORIGINAL_FILE	VARCHAR2(500)		NULL,
	RENAME_FILE	VARCHAR2(500)		NULL,
	JOIN_DATE	DATE		NULL,
	RP_COUNT	NUMBER	DEFAULT 0	NULL,
	CHAT_YN	VARCHAR(2)	DEFAULT 'Y'	NULL,
	OUT_YN	VARCHAR2(2)	DEFAULT 'N'	NULL
);

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.ID IS '아이디';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.NAME IS '이름';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.NICKNAME IS '닉네임';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.PWD IS '비밀번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.EMAIL IS '이메일';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.PHONE IS '핸드폰번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.BIRTHDAY IS '생일';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.ADDRESS IS '주소';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MAIN_NO IS '메인 번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.ORIGINAL_FILE IS '수정 전 사진명';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.RENAME_FILE IS '수정 후 사진명';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.JOIN_DATE IS '가입날짜';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.RP_COUNT IS '신고 누적 횟수';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.CHAT_YN IS '채팅 가능 여부';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.OUT_YN IS '탈퇴여부';

DROP TABLE MAIN;

CREATE TABLE MAIN (
	MAIN_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	CATEGORY	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL
);

COMMENT ON COLUMN MAIN.MAIN_NO IS '메인화면 번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MAIN.CATEGORY IS '카테고리';

DROP TABLE MONTHLY_PLAN;

CREATE TABLE MONTHLY_PLAN (
	MP_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	ID	VARCHAR2(50)		NOT NULL,
	MP_TITLE	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	MP_START	DATE	NULL,
	MP_END	DATE	NULL,
	MP_TIME	VARCHAR2(50)		NULL,
	MP_COLOR	VARCHAR2(50)	NULL,
	MP_MAIN	VARCHAR2(500)	NULL,
	MP_SUB	VARCHAR2(500)	NULL,
	MP_MEMO	VARCHAR2(500)		NULL,
	MP_DELETE	VARCHAR2(2)	DEFAULT 'N'	NULL,
	MEMO_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	MP_VIEW	VARCHAR2(2)		NULL
);

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_NO IS '번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.ID IS '작성자 아이디';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_TITLE IS '제목';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_START IS '시작 날짜';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_END IS '종료 날짜';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_TIME IS '시간';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_COLOR IS '색상';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_MAIN IS '메인 주소';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_SUB IS '서브 주소';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_MEMO IS '메모';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_DELETE IS '삭제여부';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MEMO_NO IS '메모 번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MONTHLY_PLAN.MP_VIEW IS '메모 추가여부';

DROP TABLE MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR;

CREATE TABLE MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR (
	ID	VARCHAR2(50)		NOT NULL,
	MC_FIRST	DATE		NULL,
	MC_CYCLE	NUMBER	DEFAULT 28	NULL,
	MC_PERIOD	NUMBER	DEFAULT 5	NULL,
	MC_LAST	DATE	NULL,
	MC_UPDATE	DATE	DEFAULT SYSDATE	NULL,
	MC_PRECYCLE	NUMBER	DEFAULT 28	NULL,
	MC_DELETE	VARCHAR2(50)	DEFAULT 'N'	NULL
);

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.ID IS '작성자 아이디';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_FIRST IS '첫 시작 날짜';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_CYCLE IS '주기';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_PERIOD IS '기간';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_LAST IS '최근 시작 날짜';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_UPDATE IS '수정 날짜';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_PRECYCLE IS '이전 주기';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MENSTRUAL_CALENDAR.MC_DELETE IS '삭제여부';

DROP TABLE GROUP_PLAN;

CREATE TABLE GROUP_PLAN (
	GP_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	G_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	GM_NO	NUMBER		NOT NULL,
	GP_TITLE 	VARCHAR2(100)		NULL,

	RP_NO	NUMBER	NOT NULL,
	REPORT_ID	VARCHAR2(50)	NOT NULL,
	REPORTED_ID	VARCHAR2(50)	NOT NULL,
	RP_DATE	DATE	DEFAULT SYSDATE	NULL,
	RP_CON	VARCHAR2(500)	NULL,
	RP_CHAT	VARCHAR2(300)	NULL,
	RPR_NO	NUMBER	DEFAULT 1	NOT NULL,
	RP_RDATE	DATE	NULL,
	RP_COUNT	NUMBER	DEFAULT 0	NULL
);

COMMENT ON COLUMN REPORT.RP_DATE IS '신고 날짜';
COMMENT ON COLUMN REPORT.RP_CON IS '신고 내용';
COMMENT ON COLUMN REPORT.RP_CHAT IS '대화 내용';
COMMENT ON COLUMN REPORT.RPR_NO IS '처리 번호';
COMMENT ON COLUMN REPORT.RP_RDATE IS '처리 날짜';
COMMENT ON COLUMN REPORT.RP_COUNT IS '누적 횟수';

ALTER TABLE ONETOONE_LIST ADD CONSTRAINT PK_ONETOONE_LIST PRIMARY KEY (
	OL_NO,
	CO_NO
);


--오픈채팅--
ALTER TABLE CHAT_MULTI ADD CONSTRAINT PK_CHAT_MULTI PRIMARY KEY (
	CM_NO
);
ALTER TABLE MULTICHAT_LIST ADD CONSTRAINT PK_MULTICHAT_LIST PRIMARY KEY (
	ML_NO
);

ALTER TABLE REPORT ADD CONSTRAINT PK_REPORT PRIMARY KEY (
	RP_NO
);

ALTER TABLE REPORT_RESULT ADD CONSTRAINT PK_REPORT_RESULT PRIMARY KEY (
	RPR_NO
);


-- BOOKMARK --
ALTER TABLE BOOKMARK_LIST ADD(BL_COLOR VARCHAR2(20));

-- BOOKMAR MAP --
ALTER TABLE MAP_BOOKMARK MODIFY (MB_TIME VARCHAR2(500));
ALTER TABLE MAP_BOOKMARK MODIFY (MB_MEMO VARCHAR2(500));

-- DAILY RECORD --
ALTER TABLE DAILY_RECORD ADD(DR_THUMBNAIL VARCHAR2(100));
ALTER TABLE DAILY_RECORD MODIFY (DR_CON VARCHAR2(4000));

-- DAILY RECORD PHOTO --
ALTER TABLE DAILY_RECORD_PHOTO ADD(DRP_DELETE VARCHAR2(2) DEFAULT 'N');
